## Papar Information
- Title:  `paper name`
- Authors:  `A`,`B`,`C`
- Preprint: [https://arxiv.org/abs/xx]()
- Full-preprint: [paper position]()
- Video: [video position]()

- python
- pytorch
- numpy

- for train

  python train.py
  ```
- for test
  ```
  python test.py
  ```

|        |—— rootReducer.jsx
|        |—— usersReducer.jsx
|    |—— store
|        |—— store.js
|—— vite.config.js
```
